<text>Overall, Lollicup is great at what it offers. Though the menu isn't as exotic as next door's Tapioca Express, the options they do have are FRESH (new store design as of Oct. 2014). Tiffany and June are the go to girls at Lollicup for sure. They have been there for quite some time and know how to make each drink special.

Though they no longer offer my personal favorite (Japanese Baked Green Milk Tea), I now settle for a jasmine green milk tea since it tastes very similar. Also, they offer happy hour through out the weekdays from 5-8 were you can get BOGO on select drinks! One thing to keep in mind though, it is CASH ONLY sadly.< /text>< Response>

<date>1611010394315< /date><Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
I have improved my review because I like their Pan Dulce. I CRAVE it.  It is the best in the area.  I still probably wouldn't order a cake here due to communication issues, but the product they produce is EXCELLENT.

If they could get their process down for non-Spanish speakers to get an accurate cake order, I would improve my rating.

For the best Pan Dulce in the area, I recommend this place.

Old review
The 2 stars are for my family's cake order. Ordered a Tres Leche cake ahead of time and requested Happy Birthday to be written on it. When we went to pick up the order, there was no writing on cake and no way for anyone to do so. We left with a cake with no writing for a birthday the same day. üòï

This place would get 5 stars for the quality of their baked goods ( the best Tres Leche cake I have had and the bread and conchas are on point), but not for fulfilling a proper cake order.

It helps to know Spanish when walking into this establishment.</Review>

<Review>Visiting family and in town. We went here for the first time, it was so beautiful! Fun place to bring the whole family and little kids. The kids were running and playing in the fenced area, there are horses, a stage for musicians who perform at the winery. There was no musicians the day we went, but the kids were playing on the stage and taking photos. It was so adorable. I would go back, beautiful scenery and awesome staff!</Review></record>

<Review>Jessie's Grove is a farm first and foremost. It's been around since the mid 1800's. They've got some beautiful old buildings and even a collection of old farming equipment that you can see upon request. They also have some very old vine grapes that make for mature wine. Try the carignane. I'm not very familiar with this French varietal, but you'll get a really good taste of it here. Just don't expect this to be like an Italian resort. It's a farm and that's where all the charm lies.< /Review>< pictures>

<rating>5<//rating><Text>Jessie‚Äôs Grove Winery In Lodi, California is, without a doubt, a priceless gem for many reasons.

Since it is a winery, let‚Äôs start with the wines. One word: Delicious. Here‚Äôs some more words: Crafted with care, pride and love. Every single bottle.

From rich robust ancient vine Zinfandels to wispy Pinot Noirs, from oaky Chardonnays to seemingly honey-laden Moscatos, this winery offers palate pleasing wines.

They are a vineyard. Surrounded by acres of vines, as you drive down their olive tree lined lane you‚Äôre hit with a feeling that you are definitely entering a special place.

The dedication of over 130 years of careful grape cultivation emanates from the soil itself.   The lineage of this effort flourishes up to the moment as this vineyard is ‚ÄúHome to the oldest Zinfandel producing wines in the Lodi Appellation.‚Äù

When visiting, you are immersed in a country farm. Barns, animals, tractors, wagons and implements are everywhere you look. There are stories either of history or of use for all that you see.

Their tasting room has photos displaying the heritage of the vineyard and of the family owners. Merchandise and memorabilia is all about.

As prized as the wine certainly is, so are the people here. From the family members to the ‚Äúseems like family‚Äù employees all are open, friendly, down to earth personalities who add their own unique touches to make a visit to Jessie‚Äôs Grove amazingly special.

I am in love with this outdoor winery. Don‚Äôt worry, the tasting room is indoors.

Please be sure to visit the spacious canopied outdoor sitting and mingling area. Here you can learn of the fascinating history of the family, farm and vineyard from the family matriarch herself! She‚Äôs not always there, but count yourself lucky if she is.

Make a visit to Jessie‚Äôs Grove mandatory. You‚Äôll thank yourself for making that choice.< /Text>< pics>

< user_name>
jason mills</user_name>
< text>
My first thought on the first visit was "this place would KILL in the Manhattan Beach village" but now I love and appreciate it even more exactly because it's *NOT* in the village!

After driving past wondering about Barsha for so long I've been in several times now and realized quickly all the 5 star reviews are real. There's nothing not to love: the retail side is a surprisingly interesting and well-curated wine selection, with a lot of European, old-world, and esoteric stuff that you will absolutely NOT find anywhere else in the South Bay. Also some craft beers, outstanding whiskey and spirits section, quirky gifts, Riedel stemware, and killer cheeses and charcuterie to take home--which brings us the the "other" side of the room: the tasting and munchies bar.

The 4-selection wine flights, half glasses, and full glasses available are ALL great and change monthly.  The owner and chief pourer Adnen has fantastic taste and knowledge and chooses these carefully, and so far I've loved every single selection. But the munchies..... wow, not your everyday cheapo cheese and crackers. They surprised the hell out of me with the super high quality of cheeses, charcuterie, p√¢t√©s, homemade dips, and broiled warm baguette pieces drizzled liberally with Tunisian olive oil that makes me hungry just thinking about it.

But most importantly everyone is nice! The staff is super friendly which must be a reflection of Adnen and his wife Lenora. Adnen is probably going to be the warmest and most engaging owner you'll ever meet in ANY business. It's a great and laid back vibe and it just always feels good in there. Pop in soon and I'm sure you'll agree. 5 stars well earned!<//text>
